It not only requires agreement on the file format but also how the conversion of internal logical data formats to a flawless working practice goes. How to use the format is the key to the success of SIE.\r\n\r\nThe initial motivation for the SIE group was the exchange of information with income tax reporting programs and pre-system import such as wages, inventories, payments and receivables.
